arkakṣīreṇa dhānyābhraṃ yāmaṃ piṣṭvā tathāndhrayet  Rrā 
kapotākhye puṭe pacyātpunarmardyaṃ punaḥ pacet 
evaṃ viṃśapuṭaiḥ pakvaṃ tadabhraṃ ṣoḍaśāṃśakam  Rrā 
śuddhasūte pradātavyaṃ pakvamūṣodareṇa tat 
arkapatradravaiḥ pūrvaṃ ruddhvā svedyaṃ dinatrayam  Rrā 
tuṣāgninā prayatnena samuddhṛtyātha nikṣipet 
tasminnabhraṃ dravaṃ caiva dattvā tadvatpacet tryaham  Rrā 
ityevaṃ jārayetsūte yāvattulyābhrakaṃ bhavet 
tilaparṇīrasenaiva tatsūtaṃ cābhrakaṃ punaḥ  Rrā 
mardayettaptakhalve tu yāvadbhavati golakaḥ 
pṛthaksūtena tulyena gandhapiṣṭīṃ tu kārayet  Rrā 
stambhitā gandhapiṣṭī yā gandhajāraṇavarjitā 
tatpiṣṭī svarṇapiṣṭī ca rasābhraṃ golakaṃ tathā  Rrā 
samāṃśaṃ tritayaṃ mardyaṃ dravaiḥ kārpāsajairdinam 
tadgolaṃ vartulaṃ kṛtvā vastre baddhvātha śoṣayet  Rrā 
pācayed gandhatailaṃ tu yāvatkuṅkumasaṃnibham 
saṃjātaṃ tatsamuddhṛtya piṣṭvā nirguṇḍijairdravaiḥ  Rrā 
tenaiva cāṣṭamāṃśena nāgapatrāṇi lepayet 
piṣṭvā kārpāsapatrāṇi tatkalkena ca lepayet  Rrā 
nāgapatrāṇi ruddhvātha bhūdharākhye puṭe pacet

śatavedhikalkaḥ
mṛtavajrasya bhāgaikaṃ śuddhasūtasya ṣoḍaśa 
devadālīśaṅkhapuṣpīrasair mardyaṃ dinatrayam  Rrā 
vajramūṣāgataṃ ruddhvā dinaikaṃ bhūdhare pacet 
samuddhṛtyātha taddrāvairdinaṃ mardyaṃ nirudhya ca  Rrā 
dinaikaṃ bhūdhare pacyāt tadvanmardyaṃ ca pācayet 
ityevaṃ saptadhā kuryājjāyate bhasmasūtakam  Rrā 
tadbhasmasūtakaṃ tulyaṃ vajramūṣāndhitaṃ dhamet 
tat khoṭaṃ jāyate divyaṃ rañjayettannigadyate  Rrā 
tīkṣṇaṃ śulbaṃ samaṃ cūrṇya aṃdhamūṣāgataṃ dhamet

pūrvavatkramayogena puṭāndadyāccaturdaśa 
anena pūrvakhoṭaṃ tu drutaṃ vāpyaṃ punaḥ punaḥ  Rrā

gaṃdhakaṃ śatadhā bhāvyaṃ vanaśigruśiphādravaiḥ 
jambīrairnavasāraṃ vā bhāvitaṃ syādviḍaṃ pṛthak  Rrā 
viḍa vaḍavānala
vāsakairaṃḍakadalī devadālī punarnavā 
vāsāpālāśaniculaṃ tilaṃ kāñcanamokṣakam  Rrā 
etān samūlān ādāya nātiśuṣkān vikhaṇḍayet 
pañcāṅgaṃ mūlakaṃ dagdhvā tilakāṇḍaṃ ca tatsamam  Rrā 
etatkṣāraiḥ pūrvakalkaṃ mūtravargeṇa bhāvayet 
vastrapūtaṃ dravaṃ pacyāt mṛdvagnau lohapātrake  Rrā 
bāṣpāṇāṃ budbudānāṃ ca bahūnām udgamo yadā 
tadā kāsīsaṃ saurāṣṭrī kṣāratrayaṃ kaṭutrayam  Rrā 
gaṃdhakaṃ paṃcalavaṇaṃ navasāraṃ ca hiṃgulam 
eteṣāṃ nikṣipeccūrṇaṃ tasminpātre'tha cālayet  Rrā 
guḍapākaṃ samuttārya lohasaṃpuṭake kṣipet 
saptāhaṃ bhūmigarbhe'tha dhānyarāśau tathā punaḥ 
saptāhaṃ saṃsthitaḥ siddho viḍo'yaṃ vaḍavānalaḥ  Rrā 
viḍa for sattvajāraṇa
bhāvayenniculakṣāraṃ devadālīdaladravaiḥ 
ekaviṃśativāraṃ tu biḍo'yaṃ sattvajāraṇe  Rrā 
viḍa tīvrānala
devadālīśiphābījaṃ guṃjāsaiṃdhavaṭaṃkaṇam 
samāṃśaṃ niculakṣāramamlavargeṇa saptadhā  Rrā 
kośātakīdalarasairbhāvayeddinasaptakam 
tīvrānalo nāma biḍo vihito hemajāraṇe  Rrā 
viḍa for jāraṇa of gold
mūlakārdrakavahnīnāṃ kṣāraṃ gomūtralolitam 
vastrapūtaṃ dravaṃ grāhyaṃ gaṃdhakaṃ tena bhāvayet  Rrā 
śatavāraṃ khare gharme viḍo'yaṃ hemajāraṇe  Rrā 
viḍa for jāraṇa of gold
trikṣāraṃ paṃcalavaṇaṃ śaṅkhaṃ tālaṃ manaḥśilā 
dinaikamamlavargeṇa pakvaṃ syāddhemajāraṇe  Rrā 
viḍa for jāraṇa of gold
gaṃdhakaṃ navasāraṃ ca jambīrāmlena mardayet 
śatavāraṃ khare gharme biḍo'yaṃ hemajāraṇe  Rrā 
viḍa for jāraṇa
kanyāhayāridhattūradravairbhāvyaṃ tu gaṃdhakam 
śatadhā taṃ khare gharme viḍo'yaṃ sarvajāraṇe  Rrā 
anena grasate śīghraṃ śuktisaṃbhavasaṃpuṭe  Rrā 
viḍa for improvement of grāsana
saiṃdhavaṃ gaṃdhakaṃ tulyaṃ tāmravallīdravaiḥ plutam 
anena biḍayogena gaganaṃ grasate rasaḥ  Rrā 
siddhaviḍa
śilāgaṃdhakasindhūtthaṃ pratyekaṃ ca palaṃ palam 
palatrayaṃ ca bhūnāgaṃ sarvamekatra mardayet  Rrā 
śoṣayecca punardeyaṃ bhūnāgānāṃ palatrayam 
tadvanmardyaṃ punaḥ śoṣyaṃ pācayenmandavahninā  Rrā 
evam aṣṭaguṇaṃ dattvā mardyaṃ pācyaṃ vicūrṇayet 
ayaṃ siddhaviḍo yojyo jāraṇe hemakarmaṇi  Rrā 
samyak saṃskṛtagaṃdhakādyuparasaṃ sattvaṃ tato vyomajaṃ paścānmākṣikasattvahāṭakavaraṃ garbhadrutau drāvitam 
rāgai rañjitabījajālam akhilaṃ bāhyāṃ drutiṃ dvaṃdvitāṃ sūte sarvamidaṃ krameṇa vidhinā siddhairbiḍairjārayet  Rrā 
RRĀ  
rasasya  saṃskārāḥ
siddhaiḥ sūtavarasya karma vividhaṃ khyātaṃ vicitraiḥ kramaiḥ sādhyāsādhyavivekato hy anubhavan dṛṣṭvā samastaṃ mayā 
yuktyāṣṭādaśadhā viśeṣavidhinā svedādivedhāntakaṃ dakṣāṇāṃ sukhasādhyameva sukhadaṃ saṃtanyate sāmpratam  Rrā 
 saṃskāras
svedanaṃ mardanaṃ mūrchotthāpanaṃ pātanaṃ tridhā 
nirodhanaṃ niyāmaśca dīpanaṃ cānuvāsanam  Rrā 
jāraṇaṃ cāraṇaṃ caiva garbhabāhyadrutis tathā 
rañjanaṃ sāraṇaṃ cānusāraṇā pratisāraṇā krāmaṇaṃ dehaloheṣu  Rrā 
kāñjika production
nānādhānyairyathāprāptais tuṣavarjair jalānvitaiḥ 
mṛdbhāṇḍaṃ pūritaṃ rakṣedyāvadamlatvamāpnuyāt  Rrā 
tanmadhye bhṛṅgarāṅmuṇḍī viṣṇukrāntā punarnavā 
mīnākṣī caiva sarpākṣī sahadevī śatāvarī  Rrā 
triphalā girikarṇī ca haṃsapādī ca citrakam 
samūlaṃ khaṇḍayitvā tu yathālābhaṃ niveśayet  Rrā 
pūrvāmlabhāṇḍamadhye tu dhānyāmlakamidaṃ bhavet 
kāñjka use
svedanādiṣu sarvatra rasarājasya yojayet 
kāñjika substituted by āranāla
atyamlam āranālaṃ vā tadabhāve niyojayet  Rrā 
svedanam
tryūṣaṇaṃ lavaṇaṃ rājī citrakaṃ triphalārdrakam 
mahābalā nāgabalā meghanādaḥ punarnavā  Rrā 
meṣaśṛṅgī citrakaṃ ca navasāraṃ samaṃ samam 
etat samastaṃ vyastaṃ vā pūrvāmlenaiva mardayet  Rrā 
tatkalkena limped vastre yāvad aṅgulamātrakam 
tanmadhye nikṣipetsūtaṃ baddhvā pacyāddinatrayam 
dolāyantre 'mlasaṃyukte svedito jāyate rasaḥ  Rrā 
mardanam
prakṣālya kāñjikaiḥ soṣṇais tamādāya vimardayet 
atyamlam āranālaṃ tattadabhāve niyojayet  Rrā 
gṛhadhūmeṣṭikācūrṇaṃ dagdhorṇā lavaṇaṃ guḍam 
rājikā triphalā kanyā citrakaṃ bṛhatī kaṇā  Rrā 
vandhyākarkoṭakī cātha vyastaṃ vātha samastakam 
kvāthayedāranālena tena mardyaṃ tryahaṃ rasam 
prakṣālya kāñjikenaiva samādāya vimūrchayet  Rrā 
mūrchanam
meṣaśṛṅgī kṛṣṇadhūrto balā śvetāparājitā  Rrā 
kanyāgnitriphalā caiva sarpākṣī sūraṇaṃ vacā 
gojihvā cāṅgulī nīlī muruṇḍī kṣīrakandakam  Rrā 
rājikā kākamācī ca ravikṣīraṃ ca kāñcanam 
vyastānāṃ vā samastānāṃ drāvaiścaiṣāṃ vimardayet  Rrā 
yāmaikaṃ rasarājaṃ ca mūṣāyāṃ saṃnirodhayet 
puṭaikena pacettaṃ tu bhūdhare vātha mardayet  Rrā 
sarvadrāvair yathāpūrvaṃ ruddhvā ruddhvā vipācayet 
ityevaṃ saptadhā kuryājjāyate mūrchito rasaḥ  Rrā 
utthāpanam
jalaiḥ soṣṇāranālair vā lolanādutthito bhavet 
athavā pātanāyantre pācanādutthito bhavet 
evamutthāpitaḥ sūtastridhā pātyaḥ krameṇa tu  Rrā 
ūrdhvapātanam
kākamācī jayā brāhmī cāṅgerī raktacitrakam 
aṅkolī rājavṛkṣaśca tilaparṇī kumārikā  Rrā 
maṇḍūkī citrakaṃ pāṭhā kākajaṅghā śatāvarī 
bhūpāṭalī devadālī nirguṇḍī girikarṇikā  Rrā 
śaṇapuṣpyārdrakaṃ śṛṅgī gojihvā kṣīrakandakam 
nīlī caiṣāṃ samastānāṃ vyastānāṃ ca dravairdinam  Rrā 
tāmrapādayutaṃ sūtaṃ mardayedamlakaiḥ saha 
tatpiṣṭaḥ pātayedyantre cordhvapātanake punaḥ  Rrā 
ādāya mardayettadvattāmracūrṇena saṃyutam 
pātayenmardayeccaiva tāmraṃ dattvā punaḥ punaḥ 
ityevaṃ saptadhā kuryānmardanaṃ pātanaṃ kramāt  Rrā 
ūrdhvalagnaṃ samādāya adhaḥpātena pātayet  Rrā 
adhaḥpātanam
triphalā rājikā śigrustryūṣaṃ lavaṇacitrakam 
sūtatulyaṃ tu tatsarvaṃ kāñjikair mardayeddinam  Rrā 
tena limped ūrdhvabhāṇḍaṃ pṛṣṭhe deyaṃ puṭaṃ laghu 
adhaḥpātanayantre tu pātitaṃ tu samuddharet  Rrā 
tiryakpātanam
triphalā rājikā śigrustryūṣaṃ lavaṇacitrakam 
dhānyābhrakaṃ rasaṃ sarvaṃ mardayedāranālakaiḥ  Rrā 
naṣṭapiṣṭaṃ tu tat pātyaṃ tiryagyantre dṛḍhāgninā  Rrā 
nirodhanam
lavaṇenāmbupiṣṭena haṇḍikāntargataṃ rasam 
ācchādyātha jalaṃ kiṃcit kṣiptvā śrāveṇa rodhayet 
ūrdhvaṃ laghupuṭaṃ deyaṃ labdhvāpyadho bhavedrasaḥ  Rrā 
dīpanam
trikṣāraṃ pañcalavaṇaṃ bhūkhagaṃ śigrumūlakam 
svarṇapuṣpī ca kāsīsaṃ maricaṃ rājikā madhu  Rrā 
kṣīrakando jayā kanyā vijayā girikarṇikā 
kākajaṅghā śoṇapuṣpī pātālagaruḍī kaṇā  Rrā 
vandhyākarkoṭakī vahnirvyastaṃ vātha samastakam 
peṣayedamlavargeṇa taddravairmardayedrasam  Rrā 
dinānte bandhayedvastre dolāyantre tryahaṃ pacet 
pūrvadrāvairghaṭe pūrṇe grāsārthī jāyate rasaḥ  Rrā 
anuvāsanam
dīpitaṃ rasarājaṃ tu jambīrarasasaṃyutam 
dinaikaṃ dhārayed gharme mṛtpātre vāsito bhavet  Rrā 
svedanādiśubhakarmasaṃskṛtaḥ saptakañcukavivarjito bhavet 
aṣṭamāṃśam avaśiṣyate tadā śuddhasūta iti kathyate budhaiḥ  Rrā 
RRĀ  
samukhavimukhasūte jāraṇārthaṃ pravakṣye vividhasulabhayogairbhojanaṃ gaṃdhakasya 
tadanu ca ghanacūrṇairbhojanaṃ pācanaṃ syāt nikhilasūtavibhūtyai vārtikānāṃ sukhāya  Rrā 
mercur jāraṇa of sulfur
gaṃdhakaṃ sūkṣmacūrṇaṃ tu saptadhā bṛhatīdravaiḥ 
bhāvayedvātha vṛntākarasenaiva tu saptadhā  Rrā 
palaikaṃ pāradaṃ śuddhaṃ kācakūpyantare kṣipet 
karṣakaṃ bhāvitaṃ gaṃdhaṃ karpūraṃ māṣamātrakam  Rrā 
kṣiptvā tatra mukhaṃ ruddhvā mṛdā kūpīṃ ca lepayet 
dīpāgninā dinaṃ pacyānmukhamudghāṭayetpunaḥ  Rrā 
jīrṇe gaṃdhaṃ ca karpūraṃ dattvā tadvacca jārayet 
evaṃ śataguṇe jīrṇe gaṃdhakaṃ jārayedrase  Rrā 
mercury jāraṇa of sulfur
kāsīsaṃ caiva saurāṣṭrī sajjīkṣāreṇa modakam 
śigrutoyena saṃyuktaṃ kṛtvā bhāvyamanena vai  Rrā 
saptāhaṃ cūrṇitaṃ gaṃdhaṃ taṃ gaṃdhaṃ jārayetpunaḥ 
iṣṭikāgartamadhye tu samyak śuddharasaṃ kṣipet  Rrā 
mukhaṃ svacchena vastreṇa chādayettasya pṛṣṭhataḥ 
daśāṃśaṃ gaṃdhakaṃ dattvā śrāvakeṇa nirodhayet  Rrā 
pṛṣṭhe laghupuṭaṃ deyaṃ jīrṇe gaṃdhaṃ punaḥ kṣipet 
evaṃ śataguṇaṃ jāryaṃ gaṃdhakaṃ pārade śanaiḥ  Rrā 
mercury jāraṇa of pakvabīja
taṃ rasaṃ taptakhalve tu kṣipedvastreṇa gālitam 
pādāṃśakaṃ pakvabījaṃ dattvāmlairmardayeddinam  Rrā 
taṃ kṣipeccāraṇāyantre jaṃbīrarasasaṃyutam 
taṃ yaṃtraṃ dhārayed gharme jārito jāyate rasaḥ  Rrā 
mercury jāraṇa of pakvabīja
saviḍaṃ kalayedyaṃtre dinaikaṃ tu puṭe pacet 
jāritaṃ syātpunarbījaṃ dattvā jāryaṃ ca pūrvavat 
jārayecca punastadvadevaṃ jāryaṃ samaṃ kramāt  Rrā 
mercury sāraṇā with pakvabīja
jāritaṃ sāraṇāyantre kṣipettailaṃ vasānvitam 
drāvitaṃ nālamūṣāyāṃ pakvabījarasānvitam  Rrā 
tadyaṃtre dhārayedevaṃ sārito jārayedrasaḥ 
sāritaṃ tatpunarmardyaṃ pūrvavad biḍasaṃyutam  Rrā 
jārayetkacchape yaṃtre jīrṇe bīje tu sārayet 
pūrvavat sāraṇāyantre bījena dviguṇena vai  Rrā 
punastaṃ jārayettadvattathaiva pratisārayet 
triguṇena tu bījena pūrvavajjārayetpunaḥ  Rrā 
mercury mukha bandhana
tadrasaṃ tālakaṃ tulyaṃ tailaṃ dhattūrasaṃbhavam 
divyauṣadhīgaṇadrāvaṃ sarvaṃ mardyaṃ dināvadhi  Rrā 
vajramūṣāndhitaṃ pacyātkarīṣāgnau dināvadhi 
punardivyauṣadhīdrāvairmardyaṃ pācyaṃ dināvadhi 
ityevaṃ ca punaḥ kuryātsūto baddhamukho bhavet  Rrā 
rasabandhanam
taṃ rasaṃ dhautamākṣīkaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ śulbaṃ rasaḥ śaśī 
samāṃśaṃ devadālyutthadravairmardyaṃ dināvadhi  Rrā 
tridinaṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ marditaṃ golakīkṛtam 
vajramūṣāgataṃ ruddhvā śoṣyaṃ tīvrāgninā dhamet  Rrā 
khadirāṅgārayogena khoṭabaddho bhavedrasaḥ 
tatkhoṭaṃ ṭaṃkaṇaiḥ kācaiḥ śodhayedvai dhamandhaman  Rrā 
tejaḥpuñjo raso baddho bālārkasadṛśo bhavet  Rrā 
silver  gold
tadrasaṃ sikthakenaiva veṣṭayitvā prapūjayet 
śatāṃśaṃ tu drute tāre krāmaṇenaiva saṃyutam  Rrā 
tattāraṃ jāyate svarṇaṃ jāṃbūnadasamaprabham 
aṣṭānavatibhāgaṃ syādityevaṃ vedhako mataḥ  Rrā 
mercury mukhakaraṇa
atha vakṣye rasendrasya vāsitasya mukhaṃ kramāt 
yena vyomādivaikrāntaṃ caratyāśvabhiṣecitam  Rrā 
amlavetasajaṃbīrabījapūrakabhūkhagaiḥ 
tridinaṃ mardayetsūtaṃ bhūnāgaiśca dinatrayam 
taptakhalve dinaṃ mardyaṃ sūtasyetthaṃ mukhaṃ bhavet  Rrā 
mercury mukhakaraṇa
madhyagartasamāyuktaṃ kārayediṣṭikādvayam 
dhānyābhraṃ gaṃdhakaṃ śuddhaṃ pratyekaṃ daśaniṣkakam  Rrā 
yāmaṃ jambīrajairdrāvair mardyaṃ tenaiva lepayet 
gartadvayaṃ samāṃśena hyadhogartaṃ suśodhitam  Rrā 
viṃśaniṣkaṃ kṣipetsūtam ūrdhvaṃ deyāpareṣṭikā 
liptvā mṛllavaṇaiḥ saṃdhiṃ dīptāgniṃ jvālayedadhaḥ  Rrā 
avicchinnaṃ divārātrau yāvatsaptadināvadhi 
svāṃgaśītaṃ samuddhṛtya rasaṃ kiṭṭavivarjitam 
ityevaṃ tu tridhā kuryādrasasya tu mukhaṃ bhavet  Rrā 
mercury mukhakaraṇa
vaṃśanālāndhitaṃ sūtaṃ bhāṇḍe gomūtrapūrite 
trisaptāhaṃ paceccullyāṃ sūtasyetthaṃ mukhaṃ bhavet  Rrā 
parallel between saṃskāras and ritual
samukhe nirmukhe sūte vakṣyate jāraṇaṃ kramāt 
khalvapītaṃ raso liṅgaṃ mardanaṃ mārjanaṃ smṛtam  Rrā 
nānauṣadhīrasaiḥ snānaṃ sattvairbījaiḥ prapūjanam 
svarṇādiratnajātaiśca upahāraṃ prakalpayet  Rrā 
naivedyaṃ rañjanaṃ divyaṃ sāraṇā syādvisarjanam 
vedhanaṃ dehaloheṣu samyakpūjāvidheḥ phalam  Rrā 
yāvaddināni vahnau tu dhāraṇe jāryate rasaḥ 
tāvadyugasahasrāṇi śivaloke mahīyate  Rrā 
yatkiṃcidrasarājasya sādhanārthe vyayo bhavet 
tatsarvaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ datte śrī bhairavī dhruvam  Rrā 
sādhakānāṃ sudhīrāṇām iha loke paratra ca 
ato bhūpairvārtikendraiḥ sādhyaḥ syād bhuktimuktidaḥ  Rrā 
abhra preparation for cāraṇa
arkakṣīreṇa dhānyābhraṃ dinaṃ mardyaṃ nirudhya ca 
kapotākhye puṭe pacyāt kṣīrairyāmaṃ vimardayet  Rrā 
ruddhvādhaḥ pūrvavatpacyādevaṃ vāracatuṣṭayam 
tridhā ca mūlakadrāvai rambhākandadravaistridhā  Rrā 
apāmārgakākamācīmīnākṣībhṛṅgarāṇmuniḥ 
punarnavā meghanādo vidāriścitrakaṃ tathā  Rrā 
kramād eṣāṃ dravaireva mardanaṃ puṭapācanam 
ekaikenaikavāraṃ ca dattvā tadbhāvayetpunaḥ  Rrā 
śatāvarī tālamūlī kadalī taṇḍulīyakam 
arkaḥ punarnavā śigruryavaciñcā hyanukramāt  Rrā 
pratidravair dinaikaṃ tu bhāvitaṃ cāraṇe hitam  Rrā 
abhra Vorbereitung auf cāraṇa
arkakṣīraistu dhānyābhraṃ yāmaṃ mardyaṃ nirudhya ca 
kapotākhye puṭe pacyādevaṃ vārāṃścaturdaśa  Rrā 
kadalī musalī śigrurvandhyāṅkollārkapīlukam 
nāgavallī kuberākṣī bhūmyapāmārgatumbaruḥ  Rrā 
eṣāmekadravaṃ grāhyaṃ kāṃjike vyomasaṃyutam 
sarvametatkṣiped bhāṇḍe tanmadhye pācayet tryaham  Rrā 
pūrvābhraṃ dolikāyantre samuddhṛtyātha śoṣayet 
kāsīsaṃ tuvarī sindhuṣṭaṃkaṇaṃ ca samaṃ samam  Rrā 
sarvametaddaśāṃśaṃ tu kṣiptvā tasminvimardayet 
dinaikaṃ taptakhalve tu kṣiptvā tasminvimardayet  Rrā 
dinaikaṃ taptakhalve tu tadabhraṃ cāraṇe hitam  Rrā 
abhra preparation for cāraṇa
śatavāraṃ drutaṃ nāgaṃ muṇḍīdrāve vinikṣipet 
tena drāveṇa dhānyābhraṃ marditaṃ saptadhā puṭet 
mardyaṃ mardyaṃ nirudhyātha kapotākhye puṭe pacet  Rrā 
tattulyaṃ gaṃdhakaṃ dattvā pūrvoktairmuṇḍikādravaiḥ  Rrā 
sastanyair bījapūrotthair drāvairbhāvyaṃ dināvadhi 
etadabhraṃ tu sūtasya cāraṇe paramaṃ hitam  Rrā 
siddhamūlī
vyāghrapādī haṃsapādī kadalyagnikumārikāḥ 
bṛhatī lāṅgalī vajrī khaṇḍajārīndravāruṇī  Rrā 
vandhyākarkoṭakī mūṣā sarpākṣī śaṅkhapuṣpikā 
maṇḍūkī agnimathano vikhyātā siddhamūlikā  Rrā 
etāḥ samastā vyastā vā coktasthāne niyojayet  Rrā 
mercury samukha 
cāraṇa of abhra
athātaḥ samukhe sūte pūrvābhraṃ ṣoḍaśāṃśakam 
dattvā mardyaṃ taptakhalve siddhamūlīdravairdinam  Rrā 
tatastaṃ cāraṇāyaṃtre jaṃbīrarasasaṃyutam 
gharme dhāryaṃ dinaikaṃ tu caratyeva na saṃśayaḥ  Rrā 
mercury lakṣa
koṭivedhin
cāritaṃ bandhayedvastre dolāyaṃtre dināvadhi 
siddhamūlīdravairyuktaiḥ pātanājjīryate hyalam  Rrā 
ajīrṇaṃ cetpacedyaṃtre kacchapākhye dināvadhi

koṭivedhin

sahasraguṇite jīrṇe pūrvavatsāraṇātrayam

dvandvam of vyomasattva and minerals

sattva melāpana

dvandvamel lepa for

cūrṇatulyaṃ baṃgacūrṇaṃ sarvamekatra taṃ dhamet 
dvaṃdvamelāpaliptāyāṃ jātaṃ khoṭaṃ vicūrṇayet  Rrā 
amlapiṣṭaṃ puṭe pacyādityevaṃ paṃcadhā puṭet 
taccūrṇaṃ vāhayettāre yāvaddaśaguṇaṃ dhamet  Rrā 
tattāraṃ rasarājasya samaṃ jāryaṃ krameṇa vai 
pūrvavacca tridhā sāryaṃ śatavedhī bhavedrasaḥ  Rrā 
copper  silver
evaṃ sattvābhrasattvaṃ ca cūrṇaṃ dvaṃdvaṃ ca pūrvavat 
pādāṃśaṃ tālakaṃ dattvā amlaiḥ piṣṭvā nirudhya ca  Rrā 
pacetpañcapuṭairevaṃ tāre vāhyaṃ dviṣaḍguṇam 
etadbījaṃ samaṃ jāryaṃ pratyekaṃ daśabhāgakam  Rrā 
baṃgaṃ śvetābhrasattvaṃ ca pratyekaṃ daśabhāgakam 
tārākhyā vimalā tīkṣṇaṃ pratyekaṃ pañcabhāgikam  Rrā 
dvaṃdvamelāpaliptāyāṃ mūṣāyāṃ taṃ dhamed dṛḍham 
amlapiṣṭaṃ puṭe pācyaṃ pañcavāraṃ punaḥ punaḥ  Rrā 
tadvāhyaṃ tārabhāgasya tāracūrṇaṃ kṣipan kṣipan 
tadbījaṃ rasarājasya jāryaṃ śataguṇaṃ kramāt  Rrā 
sārayettārabījena vidhinā sāraṇātrayam 
anenaivāyutāṃśena drutaṃ tāmraṃ tu vedhayet 
jāyate rajataṃ divyaṃ śaṃkhakundendusannibham  Rrā 
itthaṃ rase kanakabījamanantayogaiḥ kṛtvā bhiṣak tamakhilaṃ vidhivacca jāryam 
tenaiva hemanicayaṃ rajataṃ ca kṛtvā dāridryadāhamakhileṣu janeṣu kuryāt  Rrā

bīja preparation
gaṃdhakaṃ mākṣikaṃ nāgaṃ sarvaṃ tulyaṃ vicūrṇayet 
triguṇaṃ vāhayetsvarṇaṃ drāvitaṃ tu dhaman dhaman  Rrā

bīja preparation
nāgaṃ svarṇaṃ samaṃ tāpyaṃ śilācūrṇaṃ kṣipan kṣipan 
jīrṇe nāge punardeyam evaṃ vāratrayaṃ śanaiḥ 
etad bījaṃ dravatyeva rasagarbhe tu mardanāt  Rrā 
bījasādhanam 
tāpyasattvaṃ suvarṇaṃ ca dhamettāpyaṃ kṣipankṣipan 
ityevaṃ triguṇaṃ vāhyaṃ tāpyasattvaṃ ca hāṭake 
tadbījaṃ rasarājasya garbhe dravati tatkṣaṇam  Rrā 
bījasādhana 
tāpyasattvaṃ suvarṇaṃ ca samāṃśaṃ drāvayettataḥ

bījasādhana

anena svarṇapatrāṇi liptvā liptvā dhamed dṛḍham  Rrā 
drutaṃ ca vāpayettaṃ tu saptavāraṃ punaḥ punaḥ 
etadbījaṃ rasendrasya garbhe dravati mardanāt  Rrā 
bījasādhana

etatkarṣadvayaṃ tasyāḥ kācakūpyāṃ vinikṣipet  Rrā 
varṣopalāstu tenaiva lālayitvā supācite 
madhūkatailamadhye tu kṣaṇaṃ paktvā samuddharet 
jāyante padmarāgāṇi divyatejomayāni ca  Rrā 
indranīlakaraṇam
nīlīcūrṇaṃ palaikaṃ tu pūrvakūpyāṃ tu taddravam 
taddravaṃ dvipalaṃ cūrṇe kṣiptvā sarvaṃ vilolayet  Rrā 
kṣiptvā varṣotpalāṃstena pūrvatailagatānpacet 
indranīlāni tānyeva jāyante nātra saṃśayaḥ  Rrā 
marakatamaṇikaraṇam
mañjiṣṭhāṃ tālakaṃ nīlī samacūrṇaṃ prakalpayet 
kācakūpyāṃ sthitairdrāvaiḥ sarvametat sulolayet  Rrā 
varṣotpalāṃstu tenaiva siktvā pacyācca pūrvavat 
sarve marakatāstena samīcīnā bhavanti vai  Rrā 
gomedamaṇikaraṇam
mañjiṣṭhāyāḥ kaṣāyeṇa peṣayenmatsyakajjalam 
varṣotpalāṃstu tenaiva siktvā pacyācca pūrvavat  Rrā 
gomedāni tu tānyeva pravartante na saṃśayaḥ  Rrā 
puṣparāgakaraṇam
piṣṭvā tālakatulyaṃ tu jalaike rasakuṅkumam 
tanmadhye cāṣṭamāṃśaṃ tu kṣipenmatsyotthakajjalam  Rrā 
tatsarvaṃ pācayedyāmam avatārya surakṣayet 
varṣopalāṃstu tenaiva siktānpacyācca pūrvavat 
bhavanti puṣparāgāste yathā khanyutthitāni ca  Rrā 
nīlamāṇikyakaraṇam
nīlīcūrṇasya tulyāṃśaṃ kṣipenmatsyotthakajjalam 
bījakāṣṭhaṃ ca tulyāṃśaṃ jale sthāpyaṃ dināvadhi  Rrā 
tatsarvaṃ pācayedyāmamavatārya surakṣayet 
varṣopalāṃstu tenaiva siktāḥ pacyācca pūrvavat 
nīlamāṇikyasadṛśāste bhavanti na saṃśayaḥ  Rrā 
muktākaraṇam 
proktāni raṅgadravyāṇi kācakūpyāṃ pṛthak pṛthak 
rakṣayitvā prayatnena prāpte kārye niyojayet  Rrā 
sūryakāṃtasya madhye tu bilaṃ kuryāt suvartulam 
tathānyaṃ sūryakāntaṃ ca kuryādācchādane hitam  Rrā 
sūkṣmamuktāphalānyādau drāvayetpūrvayogataḥ 
taddrutaṃ sūryakāṃtasya bile pūryaṃ prayatnataḥ  Rrā 
sūryakāntenāpareṇa chāditaṃ gharmadhāritam 
yāmamātrādbhavedbaddhaṃ mauktikaṃ cātiśobhanam  Rrā 
chidraṃ kṛtvā nibadhyātha suśubhre vastrakhaṇḍake 
suśubhraistaṇḍulaiḥ sārdhaṃ kaṇḍayet tadulūkhale  Rrā 
laghuhastena yāmaikaṃ tata uddhṛtya kṣālayet 
tvacāriṣṭaphalānāṃ tu jalena saha peṣayet 
tenaiva kṣālite muktāphalaṃ bhavati śobhanam  Rrā 
muktākaraṇam 
mauktikāni susūkṣmāṇi cūrṇitāni vinikṣipet 
prasūtāyā iḍāyāstu sadyaḥ kṣīraiḥ kṣaṇāvadhi  Rrā 
tenaiva vartulākārā guṭikāḥ kārayettataḥ 
kācapātre sthitāḥ śoṣyāḥ chāyāyāṃ dinamātrakam  Rrā 
protayed aśvavālena mālāṃ kṛtvātha śoṣayet 
chāyāyāṃ kaṭhinā yāvattāvatsthāpyā vilambitāḥ  Rrā 
sthūlasya kṛṣṇamatsyasya ekakaṇṭasya codarāt 
nivāryāntrāṇi tatraiva pūrvamālāṃ niveśayet  Rrā 
udaraṃ sīvayetsūtreṇaiva bhāṇḍe nirudhya tat 
māsamātrātsamuddhṛtya chāyāyāṃ śoṣayetpunaḥ  Rrā 
kaṇḍanaṃ kṣālanaṃ caiva pūrvavatkārayecchanaiḥ 
bhavanti tāni śubhrāṇi samyaṅ muktāphalāni vai  Rrā 
muktākaraṇam 
muktāśuktiṃ samādāya jalaśuktimathāpi vā 
gharṣayetpṛṣṭhabhāgaṃ tu tasya kārṣṇyāpanuttaye  Rrā 
tāḥ śubhrāścūrṇayecchlakṣṇam īḍākṣīrādipūrvavat 
kārayetkṣālanāntaṃ ca mauktikāni bhavanti vai  Rrā 
muktākaraṇam 
sadya uddhṛtya matsyasya sthūlasya cakṣuṣī haret 
ekaikaṃ bandhayedvastre īḍākṣīrairdinaṃ pacet  Rrā 
chāyāyāṃ śoṣayetpaścāt kaṇḍanaṃ kṣālanaṃ tataḥ 
kārayetpūrvavattāni mauktikāni bhavanti vai  Rrā 
pravālakaraṇam 
dagdhaśaṃkhaṃ ca daradaṃ samaṃ cūrṇaṃ prakalpayet 
prasūtāyā mahiṣyāstu pañcame divase haret  Rrā 
kṣīraṃ tenaiva tanmardyaṃ yāmaikaṃ pūrvacūrṇakam 
vartulāṃ guṭikāṃ kṛtvā protayet tāmrasūtrake  Rrā 
rambhāgarbhadalenaiva madhyamāṃguṣṭhatarjanī 
veṣṭayitvā tu tairgrāhyā gulikāstāḥ pṛthak pṛthak  Rrā 
āvartyāvartya saṃsthāpyā raṃbhāpatraiḥ prayatnataḥ 
chāyāśuṣkāḥ śubhāḥ protyās tāmrasūtreṇa vai punaḥ  Rrā 
madhukaṃ taptatailāktaṃ dhūmena svedayecchanaiḥ 
jāyate padmarāgābhaṃ pravālaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ  Rrā 
pravālakaraṇam 
dagdhaḥ śaṃkhaḥ sasindūraṃ samāṃśaṃ cūrṇayettataḥ 
kṣīraiḥ sadyaḥprasūtāyā eḍāyā mardayed dṛḍham  Rrā 
pūrayecca tṛṇotthe vā nāle vaṃśādisaṃbhave 
supakve cānnabhāṇḍe tu yavāgūvarjite kṣipet  Rrā 
ācchādya pacyānmandāgnau ghaṭikānte samuddharet 
pravālā nalikāgarbhe jāyante padmarāgavat  Rrā 
hiṅgulakaraṇam
aśuddhaṃ pāradaṃ bhāgaṃ caturbhāgaṃ ca ṭaṃkaṇam 
ubhau kṣiptvā lohapātre kṣaṇaṃ mṛdvagninā pacet  Rrā 
tasminmanaḥśilācūrṇaṃ pāradāddaśamāṃśataḥ 
kṣiptvā cālyamayodarvyā hyavatārya suśītalam  Rrā 
kṛtvātha khaṇḍaśaḥ kṣiptvā kācakūpyāṃ nirudhya ca 
vastramṛttikayā samyak kācakūpīṃ pralepayet  Rrā 
sarvato'ṅgulamānena chāyāśuṣkaṃ tu kārayet 
vālukāyaṃtragarbhe tu dvidinaṃ mṛdunāgninā  Rrā 
kramavṛddhāgninā paścātpaceddivasapañcakam 
saptāhāt tat samuddhṛtya hiṃgulaṃ syānmanoharam  Rrā 
sindūrakaraṇam 
ciṃcātvagbhasmapādāṃśaṃ drute nāge vinikṣipet 
pācayellohaje pātre lohadarvyā nigharṣayet 
caṇḍāgninā dinaikaṃ tu sindūraṃ jāyate śubham  Rrā 
sindūrakaraṇam 
raktaśākhinyapāmārgakuṭajasya tu bhasmakam 
caturthāṃśaṃ drute nāge dattvā mardyaṃ dinadvayam  Rrā 
pūrvavallohapātre tu sindūraṃ jāyate śubham  Rrā 
sindūrakaraṇam 
bhasmanā pūrvavannāgaṃ śākasya vārijasya vā 
sindūraṃ jāyate divyaṃ yatheṣṭaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ  Rrā 
sindūrakaraṇam 
palānāṃ dviśataṃ nāgaṃ drāvayellohabhājane 
samūlavāsakābhasma pādāṃśaṃ tatra nikṣipet  Rrā 
pītavarṇaṃ bhavedyāvattāvat pacyāt pracālayet 
tataḥ suśītalaṃ kṛtvā jalena cālayetpunaḥ  Rrā 
palamātrā vaṭī kṛtvā vāsābhasmopari kṣipet 
chāyāśuṣkā samāhṛtya mṛdbhāṇḍe nūtane kṣipet  Rrā 
kṣiptvā ruddhvā paceccullyāṃ nirvāte tīvravahninā 
chidraṃ kuryād bhāṇḍavaktre śalākāṃ lohajāṃ kṣipet  Rrā 
raktavarṇā yadā syātsā tāvatpacyātparīkṣayet 
sindūraṃ jāyate divyaṃ siddhayoga udāhṛtaḥ  Rrā 
saindhavakaraṇam
navabhāṇḍe palaśataṃ sāmudralavaṇaṃ kṣipet 
niṣkaṃ niṣkaṃ sūtagaṃdhau kṣiptvā caṇḍāgninā pacet  Rrā 
dviyāmānte kṣipettasmiṃllohanārācakaṃ yadi 
raktavarṇaṃ bhavettadvai tadā vahniṃ nivārayet  Rrā 
svabhāvaśītalaṃ grāhyaṃ sindhūtthaṃ lavaṇaṃ bhavet  Rrā 
suvarcalakaraṇam
āranālaṃ palaikaṃ tu dviniṣkaṃ ca suvarcalam 
māṣaikaṃ gaṃdhakaṃ piṣṭvā sarvaṃ pātre tu dhārayet  Rrā 
palaikaṃ saiṃdhavaṃ taptaṃ kṛtvā tatra niṣecayet 
punastāpyaṃ punaḥ secyaṃ dravo yāvadviśuṣyati 
suvarcalaṃ bhavettāvan nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  Rrā 
hiṅgukaraṇam 
hiṅgunāgaramekaikaṃ laśunasya paladvayam 
catuṣpalaṃ nimbabījaṃ māṣacūrṇaṃ palāṣṭakam  Rrā 
sarvatulyāṃ bilvamajjām ajākṣīreṇa peṣayet 
tatsarvaṃ bandhayed gāḍhaṃ sārdragocarmagarbhataḥ 
pakṣatrayaṃ dhānyarāśau kṣipeddhiṃgu bhavettataḥ  Rrā 
hiṅgukaraṇam 
babbūlavṛkṣaniryāsaṃ sāmudralavaṇaṃ tathā 
tvagvarjyaṃ ca kaṇā tulyaṃ meṣīkṣīreṇa peṣayet  Rrā 
asya piṇḍasya pādāṃśaṃ śuddhahiṃgu niyojayet 
tatsarvaṃ pūrvavadbaddhaṃ carmaṇā divasatrayam  Rrā 
nirvāte lambitaṃ rakṣet hiṃgu syācchuddhahiṃguvat  Rrā 
hiṅgukaraṇam 
palaikaikaṃ guḍaṃ śuṇṭhī dvikaṃ ṭaṃkaṇaguggulum 
eraṇḍabījamajjā ca tuṣavarjyaṃ paladvayam  Rrā 
nistvaṅmāṣā paladvaṃdvam ekīkṛtya prapeṣayet 
trikarṣaṃ hiṅgu tanmadhye kṣiptvā toyena lolayet  Rrā 
tatsarvaṃ pūrvavadbaddhvā saptāhāddhiṅgutāṃ vrajet  Rrā 
hiṅgukaraṇam 
dvipale śuddhahiṃgu syād eḍākṣīraṃ ca viṃśatiḥ 
godhūmamāṣayoścūrṇaṃ pratyekaṃ tu catuṣpalam  Rrā 
alābupātramadhyasthaṃ tatsarvaṃ lolitaṃ kṣipet 
chāyāśuṣkaṃ bhavettāvadyāvaddhiṃgu śubhaṃ bhavet  Rrā 
vaṅgakaraṇam 
dhattūrabījacūrṇaṃ tu vajrīkṣīreṇa bhāvayet 
śoṣyaṃ peṣyaṃ punarbhāvyam evaṃ gharme trisaptadhā  Rrā 
tadvāpyaṃ drutanāgasya daśamāṃśena dāpayet 
ḍhālayetsnukpayomadhye tadvaṅgaṃ jāyate śubham 
bhāvayed rajanīmadhye tadbaṃgaṃ jāyate śubham  Rrā 
vaṅgakaraṇam 
bhāvayedrajanīcūrṇaṃ vajrīdugdhena saptadhā 
tadvāpaṃ daśamāṃśena drute nāge pradāpayet  Rrā 
tadvāpaṃ drutanāgasya daśamāṃśena dāpayet 
tat ḍhālyaṃ triphalākvāthe punastadvacca vāpayet  Rrā 
ṭaṃkaṇaṃ navasāraṃ ca dattvā secyaṃ nṛmūtrake 
drāvitaṃ ca punarḍhālyaṃ nṛmūtre vaṅgatāṃ vrajet  Rrā 
amlavetasakaraṇam
tvagbījarahitaṃ ciṃcāphalaṃ kāṃjikasaṃyutam 
paktvā kuryādvastrapūtaṃ jambīrāmlaṃ tu tatsamam  Rrā 
cāṅgerīmātuliṃgāmlair yathāprāptaṃ samāharet 
vastrapūtaṃ tu tatsarvaṃ pacetpādāvaśeṣitam  Rrā 
saurāṣṭrī tutthakāsīsaṃ trikṣāraṃ paṭupañcakam 
mūlasāraṃ ca tulyāṃśaṃ sarvaṃ cūrṇaṃ vinikṣipet  Rrā 
pūrvapakve tu pādāṃśaṃ punarmṛdvagninā pacet 
ghanībhūtaṃ bhaved yāvaccaṭṭakenaiva cālayet 
amlavetasamityetajjāyate śobhanaṃ param  Rrā 
sāhīkaraṇam
triphalā bhṛṅgakoraṇṭabhallātakaravīrakam 
bījāmrasamameteṣāṃ samāṃśaṃ bolakajjale  Rrā 
kṣiptvā mardyaṃ tāmrapātre pañcāhājjāyate maṣī 
tālapattreṣu bhūrjeṣu likhyate paramaṃ dṛḍham  Rrā 
ghṛtakaraṇam
nārikelātphalarasaṃ grāhyaṃ bhāgacatuṣṭayam 
tanmadhye ghṛtamekaṃ tu kṣiptvā bhāṇḍe vilolayet  Rrā 
śatāṃśena kṣipettasmin raktaśākinimūlakam 
mṛdvagninā pacetkiṃcit tatsarvaṃ jāyate ghṛtam  Rrā 
ghṛtakaraṇam 
ghṛtaṃ toyaṃ samaṃ kṛtvā viṃśatyaṃśena cunnakam 
kṣiptvā sarvaṃ tu mṛdbhāṃḍe kṣaṇaṃ hastena mardayet 
ghṛtaṃ tajjāyate sarvaṃ na cāgniṃ sahate kvacit  Rrā 
ghṛtakaraṇam 
meṣīmedaḥ pañcapalaṃ tilatailaṃ ca tatsamam 
pacenmṛdvagninā tāvadyāvatphenaṃ nivartate  Rrā 
dviniṣkaṃ kāṃjikaṃ tasmin kṣiptvā vastreṇa cālayet 
pādāṃśaṃ ca ghṛtaṃ tasmin dadyātsarvaṃ ghṛtaṃ bhavet  Rrā 
ghṛtakaraṇam 
tilatailaṃ vipacyādau yāvatphenaṃ nivartate 
gugguluṃ nikṣipettasmin kiṃcidgaṃdhanivṛttaye  Rrā 
viṃśatyaṃśena toyasya kṣiptvā cunnaṃ vilolayet 
jalatulyaṃ pūrvatailaṃ miśrayet tatsuśītalam  Rrā 
mardayenmṛṇmaye pātre hastena kṣaṇamātrakam 
ghanībhūte ghṛtaṃ cārdhaṃ kṣiptvā sarvaṃ ghṛtaṃ bhavet  Rrā 
candanakaraṇam
saṃchedya nimbavṛkṣaṃ tu hastaikaṃ rakṣayedadhaḥ 
tasya mūrdhni bilaṃ kuryāttatraiva navaguggulum  Rrā 
pūrayettena kāṣṭhena bilaṃ ruddhvātha lepayet 
saṃdhiṃ mṛllavaṇenaiva śuṣkaṃ gajapuṭe pacet  Rrā 
svabhāvaśītalaṃ grāhyaṃ tanmūlaṃ candanaṃ bhavet  Rrā 
karpūrakaraṇam
palatrayaṃ paced bhaktaṃ samyagrājānnataṇḍulam 
tad bhaktaṃ śītalaṃ kṛtvā gavāṃ kṣīraiḥ prayatnataḥ  Rrā 
niṣkamātraṃ ca karpūraṃ kṣiptvā tasmiṃśca peṣayet 
śuṣkasya vaṃśanālasya sthūlasya tena codaram  Rrā 
lepyamaṅgulamānena chāyāśuṣkaṃ ca kārayet 
chittvātha kadalīpuṣpaṃ tanniryāsena pūrayet  Rrā 
vaṃśanālaṃ punarvastrakhaṇḍe ruddhvā ca tanmukham 
ātape tridinaṃ śoṣyaṃ bhūgarte nikhanettataḥ  Rrā 
trisaptāhāt samuddhṛtya śoṣayitvā samāharet 
karpūraṃ tasya garbhasthaṃ rakṣetkarpūrabhājane 
karpūraṃ jāyate divyaṃ yathā bījaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  Rrā 
javādīyāṅkastūrīkaraṇam
panasasyārdhaṃ pakvasya bījānyekasya khaṇḍayet 
navabhāṇḍe vinikṣipya niṣkaṃ śuṇṭhī palaṃ tathā  Rrā 
cūrṇayitvā kṣipettasmin tatsarvaṃ dravatāṃ vrajet 
tena ghṛṣṭvā kṣipettasmin caturniṣkaṃ ca candanam  Rrā 
mṛdvagnau pācayettāvadyāvad āraktatāṃ gatam 
tacchītalaṃ kācapātre kṣiptvā tasyopari kṣipet  Rrā 
campakaṃ ketakīmallījātīpuṣpāṇi tatpunaḥ 
dinaṃ śubhrapaṭe baddhvā mukhaṃ tasyaiva rakṣayet  Rrā 
tataḥ puṣpāṇi saṃtyaktvā kastūrīṃ māṣamātrakām 
māṣaikaṃ śuddhakarpūre tasminneva vinikṣipet  Rrā 
nikṣipedviṃśadaṃśena samyagjāvādikāmapi 
tatsarvaṃ mathitaṃ pūrvaṃ samyagjāvādibhājane  Rrā 
veṣṭayenmallikāpuṣpaistadbhāṃḍaṃ divasatrayam 
samyagbhavati jāvādi varṇaiḥ parimalairapi  Rrā 
kastūrīkaraṇam
madhūkatailaṃ tailaṃ vā tilotthaṃ palapañcakam 
muṇḍīdrāvaṃ daśapalaṃ sarvamekatra yojayet  Rrā 
mallikā mālatī jātī ketakī śatapattrikā 
anyāni ca sugandhīni puṣpāṇi tatra nikṣipet  Rrā 
dinaikaṃ mudritaṃ rakṣet puṣpaṃ niṣpīḍya saṃtyajet 
sikthakaṃ viṃśatirniṣkān kṣiptvā tasminpacecchanaiḥ  Rrā 
yāvattailāvaśeṣaṃ syāt karpūraṃ cārdhaniṣkakam 
niṣkaṃ mārjārajāvādiṃ kṣiptvā tadavatārayet  Rrā 
anyapātre vinikṣipya śītalaṃ tatpunaḥ pacet 
kṣaṇamātrāttaduttārya kṣipejjāvādi bhājane  Rrā 
sāndraṃ bhavati tatsarvaṃ yathā bījaṃ na saṃśayaḥ 
puṣpāṇi bakulasyaiva ratnamālāṃ samaṃ samam  Rrā 
taccūrṇamikṣudaṇḍasya kṛtanālasya codare 
kṣiptvā tasya mukhaṃ ruddhvā tanmajjābhirmṛdā punaḥ  Rrā 
puṭet tṛṇāgninā tāvadyāvadgaṃdho na dahyate 
dravanti tāni puṣpāṇi mukhaṃ bhittvā dravaṃ haret  Rrā 
kastūrīcarma nirlomaṃ mustātulyaṃ vicūrṇayet 
cūrṇasya daśamāṃśena samyak kastūrikāṃ kṣipet  Rrā 
pūrvadrāveṇa tatsarvaṃ peṣitaṃ golakīkṛtam 
kastūrīmadanākārā kiṃcitkāryā prayatnataḥ  Rrā 
tatsarvaṃ chāyayā śoṣyaṃ madanā rakṣayetpṛthak 
guṭikāḥ khaṇḍaśaḥ kṛtvā madanaiḥ saha miśrayet 
kastūrīcarmaṇā baddhvā samyaṅ mṛgamado bhavet  Rrā 
kuṇkumakaraṇam 
nārikelakapālaṃ vā ghṛṣṭaṃ vā nimbakāṣṭhakam 
yatkiṃcicchubhrakāṣṭhaṃ vā toyena saha kārayet  Rrā 
tatpādaṃ rajanī cātha tasminmadhye vinikṣipet 
gairikaṃ vā rajanyardhaṃ tatsarvaṃ kuṃkumaṃ bhavet  Rrā 
kuṅkumakaraṇam 
pālāśapuṣpajaṃ kvāthaṃ gharme dhāryaṃ tu kharpare 
viṃśatyaṃśaṃ kṣipettasmin peṣitaṃ śubhrataṇḍulam  Rrā 
taṇḍulārdhaṃ tathā cunnaṃ sarvaṃ kāṣṭhena lolayet 
ghanībhūtaṃ bhavedyāvattāvad gharme pracālayet 
tatastenaiva vaṭikāḥ kṛtvā syuḥ kuṅkumopamāḥ  Rrā 
kuṅkumakaraṇam 
pālāśapuṣpapādāṃśaṃ samyakśubhraṃ ca taṇḍulam 
piṣṭvātha vaṭikāḥ kāryā śoṣyāḥ syuḥ kuṃkumopamāḥ  Rrā 
divyadhūpa 
kramāt taraguṇaṃ kuryātkastūrī śaśikuṅkumam 
nakhamāṃsī sarjarasamustā kṛṣṇāguruḥ sitā  Rrā 
candanaṃ ca daśaitāni cūrṇitāni vimiśrayet 
cūrṇatulyairguggulubhiḥ sarvamekatra kuṭṭayet  Rrā 
stokaṃ stokaṃ kṣipettailaṃ śilāyāṃ lohamuṣṭinā 
dinamekaṃ prayatnena vartikāṃ tena kārayet  Rrā 
tadagrajvalitaṃ kuryājjvālāṃ nivārya tatkṣaṇāt 
devānāṃ divyadhūpo'yaṃ mantrāṇāṃ sādhane hitaḥ  Rrā 
divyadhūpa 
pāṣāṇabhedacūrṇaṃ tu gugguluṃ ca palaṃ palam 
māṃsī mustā nakhaṃ bolacandanāguruvālakam  Rrā 
lākṣāguḍaṃ sarjarasaṃ sitākarpūrasaṃyutam 
prati niṣkadvayaṃ cūrṇya kastūrī kuṃkumaṃ tathā  Rrā 
māṣaikaikaṃ kṣipettasmin sarvaṃ kuṭyād ulūkhale 
tilatailaṃ kṣipet kiṃcil lohadaṇḍena tad dṛḍham  Rrā 
yāmaikaṃ kuṭṭayetsiddho divyo dhūpaḥ śivoditaḥ 
devādevākaro deyaḥ pūrvavadvartakīkṛtaḥ 
sarvasaubhāgyajanakaḥ sarvamantro'ghanāyakaḥ  Rrā 
puṣpadruti
vajrīkṣīreṇa saṃyuktaṃ śuddhaṃ vastraṃ punaḥ punaḥ 
ātape śoṣitaṃ kuryādityevaṃ dinasaptakam  Rrā 
jātīpuṣpapalaikaṃ tu niṣkaṃ cūrṇitaṭaṃkaṇam 
kṣaudraṃ niṣkatrayaṃ yojyaṃ sarvamekatra lolayet  Rrā 
mṛtpātre dhārayed gharme ramye vā kācabhājane 
ācchādayettu vastreṇa jalasiktena tatkṣaṇāt  Rrā 
dravanti tāni puṣpāṇi yuñjyādyogeṣu taddravam 
anenaiva prakāreṇa puṣpāṇāṃ ca pṛthak pṛthak 
drutiḥ kāryā sugandhānāṃ gaṃdhavādeṣu yojayet  Rrā 
dhānyavṛddhikaraṇam 
mandāramūlamārdrāyāṃ bharaṇyāṃ vā kuśodbhavam 
ūrdhvaṃ saṃgrāhya yatnena dhavamālye vinikṣipet  Rrā 
pravātātimukhaṃ yattu tatkāṣṭhaṃ tu samāharet 
dhānyasya rāśigaṃ kuryāddhānyavṛddhikaraṃ param  Rrā 
dhānyavṛddhikaraṇam 
kṛkalāsasya vāmākṣi hemnāveṣṭyābhimantritam 
dhānyarāśau vinikṣipya dhānyavṛddhikaraṃ param  Rrā 
dhanadhānyavṛddhikaraṇam 
tasyaiva dakṣiṇaṃ netraṃ hemnāveṣṭya tataḥ kṣipet 
yasminkasminbhave dravye dhānye vā vṛddhikārakam  Rrā 
dravyādivṛddhikaraṇam
kṛṣṇacitrakamūlaṃ tu kṣiptaṃ yasmin suvastuni 
tatsarvaṃ cākṣayaṃ nityaṃ vyayīkṛtya na kṣīyate  Rrā 
dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ ghṛtaṃ tailaṃ suvarṇaṃ navaratnakam 
yatkiṃcid dravyajātaṃ tadakṣayyaṃ tiṣṭhati dhruvam  Rrā 
dhānyavṛddhikaraṇam 
mūlaṃ suśvetaguṃjāyā jalamadhye vinikṣipet 
tanmūlaṃ dhānyarāśau ca kṣiptvā mantravidhānataḥ  Rrā 
taddhānyaṃ vardhate nityaṃ bhakṣyamāṇaṃ sahasraśaḥ 
mantrakhaṇḍe yathā proktaṃ guñjāmūlasya sādhanam 
tathaivātra prakartavyaṃ siddhirbhavati nānyathā  Rrā 
ādau sarvadiśāntareṣu gamanaṃ kṛtvā guroḥ saṃmukhāt prāptaṃ bhaktibalena yuktividhinā sārātisāraṃ mahat 
tatsarvaṃ dhanavardhanaṃ nigaditaṃ bhūyiṣṭhamadhvāṃ kvacid bhūpānāṃ viduṣāṃ mahāmatimatāṃ vidvān bhavet pālanaiḥ  Rrā 
RRĀ  
sāṅgopāṅgam anekayoganicayaṃ sāraṃ varaṃ coddhṛtaṃ yuktaṃ pāradabandhanaṃ mṛduhaṭhāt dṛṣṭaṃ paraṃ yanmayā

pāradabandhana

pāradabandhanam

pāradabandhanam

pāradabandhanam

nṛkapāle śvetaguṃjāṃ vāpayecchuddhabhūmiṣu  Rrā 
secayetsalilaṃ nityaṃ yāvatphalavatī bhavet 
mantrapūjāṃ tataḥ kṛtvā puṣye grāhya phalāni vai  Rrā 
śuddhatāmrapalaṃ śvetaṃ viṃśatyuttarakaṃ śatam 
ekaikaṃ pūrvabījānāṃ samyagruddhvā dhamed dṛḍham  Rrā 
tattāmraṃ jāyate tāraṃ śaṃkhakundendusannibham 
tāraṃ tajjāyate svarṇaṃ suśuddhā baddharītikā  Rrā 
copper  silver
bhūnāgānāṃ rasairmardyaṃ śuddhaṃ tālaṃ dināvadhi 
tatpiṇḍaṃ haṇḍikāmadhye tālakāṃśaṃ nirodhayet  Rrā 
tāmrapatrāṇi tatpaścāt ḍhaṅkaṇena nirudhya ca 
haṃḍikā bhasmanā pūryā ruddhvā caṇḍāgninā pacet  Rrā 
pañcayāmātsamuddhṛtya niṣkaṭaṃkaṇasaṃyutam 
mūkamūṣāgataṃ dhāmyaṃ guṭikāṃ tāṃ samuddharet  Rrā 
svāṃgaśītaṃ samāhṛtya mūṣāyāṃ prakaṭaṃ dhamet 
vāratrayaṃ kṣipettasmin vaṭikāṃ vedhanānmukham  Rrā 
mukhaṃ tasya bhavettīvraṃ śuddhaṃ baṃgaṃ dravatyalam 
yadā na grasate tasmādvaṭī deyā punaḥ punaḥ  Rrā 
jīrṇe śataguṇe vaṅge tataratāmrasya dāpayet 
drutasya śatabhāgena tattāraṃ jāyate śubham  Rrā 
nāgamukhakaraṇam
gaṃdhakaṃ dhūmasāraṃ ca phaṭkarī ṭaṃkaṇaṃ samam 
eraṇḍabījamajjāpi sarveṣāṃ dviguṇā bhavet  Rrā 
bhūnāgāḥ sarvatulyāḥ syuḥ sarvamekatra mardayet 
caṇamātrā vaṭīḥ kāryā khyāteyaṃ vaḍavāmukhā  Rrā 
śuddhanāgaṃ drutaṃ kṣepyaṃ taile eraṇḍake punaḥ 
drāvyaṃ drāvyaṃ punaḥ kṣepyaṃ yāvadvāraṃ śṛtaṃ bhavet  Rrā 
punastasmindrute deyā vaṭikā vaḍavāmukhā 
dvitrivāraṃ prayatnena nāgasyetthaṃ mukhaṃ bhavet  Rrā 
grasate sarvalohāni satvāni vividhāni ca 
yadā na grasate tasmād vaṭī deyā punaḥ punaḥ  Rrā 
kaṭhinadhātormṛdūkaraṇam
madhūkapuṣpī yaṣṭīkaṃ raṃbhākaṃdaṃ ghṛtaṃ guḍam 
tilatailam ajākṣīraṃ kṣaudraṃ ca tulyatulyakam  Rrā 
tanmadhye kaṭhinaṃ dhātu tridhā siñcyāt sutāpitam 
mṛdutvaṃ yāti no citraṃ sūtrayogyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  Rrā 
kaṭhinadhātor mṛdūkaraṇam 
vasubhadrarasenātha tridhā siñcya sutāpitam 
loṇavatsphuṭito dhāturmṛduḥ syāt sikthakopamaḥ  Rrā 
kaṭhinadhātor mṛdūkaraṇam 
atisthūlasya bhekasya nivāryāntrāṇi tatra vai 
cūrṇitaṃ ṭaṃkaṇaṃ kṣiptvā tadbhāṇḍasthaṃ khanedbhuvi  Rrā 
trisaptāhaṃ samuddhṛtya tadvāpe mṛdutāṃ vrajet 
svarṇaṃ vā yadi vā raupyaṃ mṛdu syātpatrayogyakam  Rrā 
abhragrāsī rasaḥ
tṛṇajyotīyamūlena mātuliṃgarasena ca 
tridinaṃ mardayetsūtaṃ gaganaṃ grasate kṣaṇāt  Rrā 
guhyākhyasūtena nāgavedhaḥ
bhūnāgasūkṣmacūrṇaṃ tu ṭaṃkaṇena samaṃ bhavet 
taccūrṇaṃ tu drute nāge vāhyaṃ śataguṇaṃ dhaman  Rrā 
guhyākhyaṃ tadbhavetsiddhaṃ grāsaṃ tasyaiva vakṣyate 
śilāgaṃdhakamākṣīkair bhūnāgadravapeṣitaiḥ  Rrā 
mūṣāgarbhaṃ lipettena guhyākhyaṃ tatra nikṣipet 
bhuktaṃ tasminkṣipetsvarṇaṃ stokaṃ stokaṃ dhamandhaman  Rrā 
grasate bhārasaṃkhyā tu mūṣā lepyā punaḥ punaḥ 
muñcatyasau drute nāge guhyādguhyaṃ prakāśitam  Rrā 
guhyākhyasūtena vaṅgavedhaḥ
bhūnāgaṃ ṭaṃkaṇaṃ tulyaṃ sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet 
taṃ vāhayed drute baṃge yāvacchataguṇaṃ dhaman  Rrā 
tataḥ śataguṇaṃ baṃgaṃ tasyaivopari vāhayet 
stokaṃ stokaṃ dhamanneva grasate nātra saṃśayaḥ  Rrā 
guhyavaṅgakaraṇaṃ tena vedhaḥ
tālakaṃ saiṃdhavaṃ tulyaṃ bhūnāgadravapeṣitam 
mūṣāgarbhe lipettena tadbaṃgaṃ tatra nikṣipet  Rrā 
stokaṃ stokaṃ kṣipettasmin biḍaṃ dattvā dhamandhaman 
bhārasaṃkhyā grasatyevaṃ guhyavaṅgamiti smṛtam  Rrā 
drute baṃge vinikṣiptaṃ yāvatsaṃkhyā na saṃśayaḥ 
tāvad drute na saṃdehaḥ siddhayoga udāhṛtaḥ  Rrā 
kṣiptvātha māhiṣe śṛṅge mardayannagninā pacet 
niṣkamekaṃ bhavedyāvattāvanmardyaṃ kṣipan kṣipan  Rrā 
tad bhavedrasatulyaṃ tu samādāyātha tatsamam  Rrā 
guhyayogaḥ
pāradaṃ śuddhahemātha satvaṃ bhūnāgasaṃbhavam 
catvāriṃśannāgabhāgā mardyaṃ jaṃbīrajadravaiḥ  Rrā 
tadgolakaṃ viśoṣyātha kalke bhūnāgasaṃbhave 
mūṣāgarbhe vilepyādau tasyāṃ golaṃ nirodhayet  Rrā 
dhamettīvrāgninā tāvadyāvannātrāvaśeṣitam 
sarvavadgrasate datte guhyākhyaṃ yogamuttamam  Rrā 
kāmadhenuḥ 
athātaḥ sampravakṣyāmi guṭikābaṃdhamuttamam 
samajīrṇaṃ kṛtaṃ vyoma samato rasaṃ jārayet  Rrā 
ravisaṃkhyāṃśakaṃ śulbaṃ dattvā piṣṭiṃ ca kārayet 
dhānyābhrakasamaṃ gaṃdhaṃ śulbe kṣiptvā vimardayet  Rrā 
tayormūṣākṛtiṃ kṛtvā piṣṭīmadhye vimocayet 
naramāṃsena saṃveṣṭya māṣapiṣṭyā tathaiva ca  Rrā 
pacedatasītailena māsamātraṃ tu sādhakaḥ 
akṣayā kāmadhenuśca vaṅgastambhanakāriṇī  Rrā 
kāmadhenuḥ 
pārade jāryaṃ kṛṣṇābhraṃ rukmam aṣṭaguṇaṃ yadi 
rañjitaṃ gandharāgeṇa naramāṃsena veṣṭitam  Rrā 
māṣapiṣṭyā pralipyāthātasītailena pācayet 
kāmadhenuriyaṃ khyātā nāgastambhanakāriṇī  Rrā 
kāmadhenuḥ 
rasātpādāṃśakaṃ hemapiṣṭiṃ kuryācca sundarām 
vilipya kāmadhenuṃ ca nāgadrāve niyojayet  Rrā 
taṃ nāgaṃ kurute rukmaṃ vāñchitārtheṣu siddhidam 
guṭikāṃ kāmadhenuṃ tāṃ pratyahaṃ dhārayenmukhe 
śastrāstrairna ca bhidyeta divyadehamavāpnuyāt  Rrā

rañjito gandharāgeṇa samahemnā ca sārayet 
tāravedhaḥ pradātavyo divyaṃ bhavati kāṃcanam  Rrā 
lead  gold
śilayā ravidugdhena nāgapatrāṇi lepayet 
mārayetpuṭayogena divyaṃ bhavati kāṃcanam  Rrā 
sitasvarṇa  gold
meṣīkṣīrāmlavargābhyāṃ daradaṃ gharmabhāvitam 
śatadhā tatprayogena śoṣyaṃ peṣyaṃ kharātape  Rrā 
sitasvarṇasya patrāṇi liptvā liptvā puṭe pacet 
evaṃ trisaptadhā kuryād divyaṃ bhavati kāṃcanam  Rrā 
gaganagrāsaḥ
tṛṇajātīyamūlaṃ tu mātuliṅgarasena ca 
tridinaṃ mardayetsūtaṃ gaganaṃ grasate kṣaṇāt  Rrā 
siddhairgaṇaiḥ suravarai rasasiddhikāmair baddhaṃ haṭhātparamamantrabalena taiśca 
tasmād viśiṣṭam anujaiḥ kṛtamantrajāpaiḥ kāryaṃ tato rasavare varabandhanaṃ ca  Rrā
